		effect = {
			add_alteration_perk_effect = { LEVEL = 2 }

		}

	trait = patient #worm cult virtue, knew to bide his time
	trait = irritable #When Iachesis refused, Mannimarco grew belligerent and vile. He spat curses and ancient blasphemies like a Daedric beast.
	trait = education_intrigue_4
	trait = education_magic_5
	trait = arcana_good_2
	trait = lifespan_4
	trait = intellect_good_3
	trait = sign_atronach
	disallow_random_traits = yes
	
	portrait_override={
		portrait_modifier_overrides={
			custom_hair=male_hair_fp1_05
		}
	}

	# 2985.1.1 = { employer = iachesis_100 }

		effect = {
			add_character_flag = ai_will_not_convert

			add_illusion_perk_effect = { LEVEL = 4 }
			add_conjuration_perk_effect = { LEVEL = 3 }
			add_destruction_perk_effect = { LEVEL = 3 }
		}
	}

		}
	}
	3300.1.1 = { # Acquire his staff
		effect = {
			create_artifact_staff_worms_effect = {
				OWNER = root
			}
			scope:newly_created_artifact = {

			}
		}
	}
	3151.1.1 = { culture = anchoriti }
	3310.1.1 = { # Acquire his amulet
